       <img alt="Wedding Music Ideas: 50 Songs For Your Walk Down the Aisle" class="image xxxlarge " data-nid="34604637" height="1024" src="http://media4.popsugar-assets.com/files/2015/04/16/009/n/1922398/397ba828_edit_img_cover_file_845210_1427537100_Photo-Bird-Bear-OYRgKd.xxxlarge/i/Wedding-Processional-Songs.jpg" title="Wedding Music Ideas: 50 Songs For Your Walk Down the Aisle" width="846"/>
       <figcaption class="highlightable">
        <p>
         If you're planning a
         <a class="sugar-inline-link" href="http://www.popsugar.com/Wedding" target="_blank" title="Latest photos and news for wedding">
          wedding
         </a>
         soon, one of the most daunting (but fun) details to figure out is the music. We've got a
         <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Wedding-Music-Guide-29582984">
          wedding music guide
         </a>
         so you know what you have to select tunes for, but as for those tunes, we can help. We have ideas for your
         <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Wedding-First-Dance-Songs-22603522">
          first dance song
         </a>
         and the
         <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Father-Daughter-Wedding-Dance-Songs-22689117">
          father/daughter dance
         </a>
         , but what about the ceremony? Your walk down the aisle kicks off the celebration, but why settle for "Here Comes the Bride?" We have a collection of processional song suggestions that span genres, from traditional and instrumental to indie and eclectic.
        </p>

    var isTestRunning = typeof SUGAR !== 'undefined' ?  SUGAR.TestSettings.getRunTest() : false;

    window.trackerNames = [];

    
    (function () {
        window.overrideReferrer = false;
        if (window.ONSUGAR &amp;&amp; ONSUGAR.Util) {
            var cookie = ONSUGAR.Util.getCookie('sugarSSOReferrer');
            if (cookie !== null) {
                window.overrideReferrer = cookie;
                ONSUGAR.Util.deleteCookie('sugarSSOReferrer');
            }
        }

        if (isTestRunning) {
            ONSUGAR.Event.registerEventHandler('groupSelected', function() {
                SUGAR.ABTest.trackPageView();
            });
        }
    })();

    if (window.overrideReferrer) {
        ga('sugarNetworkTracker.set', 'referrer', window.overrideReferrer);
    }

            ga('sugarNetworkTracker.set', 'dimension1', 'gallery');

        ga('sugarNetworkTracker.send', 'pageview');
    }
    window.trackerNames.push('sugarNetworkTracker');

            if (isTestRunning) {
            ONSUGAR.Event.registerEventHandler('groupSelected', function() {
                ga('sugarNetworkTracker.send',  'pageview', trackingUrl);
            });
        }

    if (window.overrideReferrer) {
        ga('sugarIncTracker.set', 'referrer', window.overrideReferrer);
